- :Link[About License Bundles]{label="About License Bundles" overridedLabel="About License Bundles" spaceId docId="d5mOL3ei-tYRA6yesEARd" version="v2" docAnchorId="#About_License_Bundles" loadingMethod="dynamic" newTab="false" href="All Business Objects.mdx"}

## About Business Objects

- System business objects (such as **logonhistory**) do not support business rules and cannot be used to trigger a workflow event.
- Business object application fields (such as **LastModDateTime**) do not trigger a workflow.
- Data segregation rules do not apply to audit items, which are those business objects that start with **Audit\_**. (Do not confuse these business objects with the business objects that start with **Audit** without the underscore.)  
- Data segregation rules do not apply to pure validation business objects. Pure validation business objects are the business objects that show in the validation business object lists.

### About Roles

The table lists each business object and which roles can add, view, edit, or delete that business object. (Guests can view all business objects, but cannot add, edit, or delete any business objects. The guest role is not listed in the table below.) The list of roles is at the bottom of the table.

### About License Bundles

The final column of the table lists the license bundles associated with a business object. The following are the license bundles and how they are noted in the table:

- Help Desk (HD)
- Self Service (SS)
- Service Management (SM)
- Service Desk (SD)
- Service Catalog (SC)
- Discovery (Dis) (Some business objects are available as part of the Discovery add-on module. An add-on module is a single module that is not part of any bundle but is sold separately.)

1. Click **OK** to close the informational message.

### Role Legend

Admin - Administrator

ChM - Change Manager

ConM - Configuration Manager

DA - \{\{FRS\_VARS.Neurons\_ITSM\_-\_Discovery\_Analyst}}

DM - \{\{FRS\_VARS.Neurons\_ITSM\_-\_Discovery\_Manager}}

E - Executive

G - Guests

H - Help Desk Demo

IM - Inventory Manager

KM - Knowledge Manager

LM - License Manager

PPM - Portfolio Manager

PrbM - Problem Manager

PrjM - Project Manager

RelM - Release Manager

RepM - Report Manager

SS - Self Service

SSM - Self Service Mobile

SO - Service Owner

SDA - Service Desk Analyst

SDM - Service Desk Manager

SDACL - Support Desk Analyst for Call Log

SDMCL - Support Desk Manager for Call Log

SSCL - Self Service with Call Log
